GT: F0*sin(t) - beta*sin(x)*v

## Analysis

The Ground Truth (GT) is:
$$f(x, t, v) = 0.767518\sin(t) - 0.263896\,v\sin(x)$$

I need to find a candidate where constants can be chosen to reproduce this expression exactly.

**Candidate 1**: `c0*v*exp(c1*x) + c2*sin(c3*x + c4) + c5*x*exp(c6*x) + c7*sin(c8*t + c9)`

Setting c5=0 eliminates the `x*exp(c6*x)` term. But `c0*v*exp(c1*x)` cannot become `-0.263896*v*sin(x)` since exp cannot become sin. ❌

**Candidate 6**: `c0*x**c1 + c2 + c3*v*x**c4 + c5*sin(c6 + c7*t + c8*x**c9)`

The term `c3*v*x**c4` is a power of x times v, not `v*sin(x)`. The sin term mixes t and x. This can't separate into `sin(t)` and `v*sin(x)`. ❌

**Candidate 25**: `c0/x**5 + c1 + c2*sin(c3*t + c4)*cos(c5*x) + c6*v*x**c7 + c8*v**2*x + c9/x**3`
